Current Commentary

Implementing Land Administration 8

— Li

The conference of local senior administrative personnel has opened. Under the leadership of the Executive Yuan, senior administrative personnel from ten provinces have gathered together, and leaders with actual political responsibilities have personally delivered instructions. It cannot be denied that this is a major event in China's recent politics.

When describing the key points of the conference, President Jiang of the Executive Yuan solemnly raised the issue of land administration, saying: "We must understand that the land issue is a fundamental issue in politics, and land administration is a basic task in politics. If land administration cannot be implemented perfectly and the land issue cannot be resolved properly, political construction will not only fail to succeed but also be impossible to advance." The state of politics is originally built on economic conditions.

Before receiving the "reports on the situation of land administration preparation in various provinces," we dare not speculate on what kind of "joint resolution" this conference will make regarding the land administration issue. However, we hope that the results of this conference will definitely not start with land consolidation and end with increased taxation. Of course, no wealthy country will have a poor government. However, if the government's every move is aimed at increasing tax revenue, then the country will never become wealthy.

Solving the land issue as a fundamental political issue undoubtedly involves two major issues: one is the distribution of land to optimize the improvement of people's livelihood, and the other is the improvement of land to increase its productivity.

Many people, including some economists, believe that these two aspects can be carried out separately. The faction that values ​​land distribution believes that as long as the land is divided up so that landless poor farmers become self-cultivating farmers, the revitalization of the countryside can be expected in the near future. The faction that values ​​land improvement believes that today China only has the distinction between small poverty and great poverty, and therefore believes that increasing production is the only economic issue.

These two factions each hold a part of the truth. Without opening up wasteland or increasing land productivity, simply dividing the already cultivated land may not increase the happiness of the poor. Compared with China's total area, China's population is still sparse. However, if production technology is not improved, merely distributing the currently cultivated land to the people may not have much effect even if it is evenly distributed. Conversely, without restricting the application of land ownership, the slogan of land improvement will probably remain just a slogan in the end. Under the current situation, since the government cannot assume the responsibility of improving the land on behalf of the people, it will naturally place the responsibility of improvement on the people themselves. However, it must be understood that cultivators without land ownership have no intention of improving the land, and land owners who do not cultivate the land have even less intention of improving the land.

We believe that the work of land distribution must be carried out together with the work of land improvement. It is true that what the current government needs is not a revolution in land ownership. However, allowing the poor who have no land but have the ability to cultivate to open up and improve unused land, or at least unmanaged land, without compensation, and fully guaranteeing their interests is the minimum work in the land administration issue. If even this cannot be discussed, then it is not known what other significance the land administration issue has.

The prerequisite for this kind of work is definitely not funding. The biggest reason why all measures in China have no significant effect is the problem of having only institutions without work. The establishment of several land administration agencies can at most support a few intellectuals.

The prerequisite for this kind of work is the decision of a fundamental economic policy. If the government truly has the determination to fulfill its mission—Article 120 of the draft constitution: "The state shall, in principle, allocate and consolidate land to support self-cultivating farmers and those who use land themselves"—then all it needs to do is remove the obstacles to this kind of work. Specifically, it only needs to facilitate the migration of farmers, so that the nominal owners of land dare not obstruct the intrusion of actual cultivators, and to guarantee the benefits obtained by farmers through labor, so that the land has the possibility of being improved.

Administrative Yuan Passes Measures for the Ministry of Industries' Fisheries Syndicate, Submits a Request to the National Government for Commendation of Ding Wenjiang, Appoints Guo Taiqi as Representative for Treaty Negotiations with Latvia, and Appoints Wang Jingqi as Minister to Sweden and Norway 9

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held its 262nd regular meeting on the morning of the 12th. Those present were Chiang Kai-shek, Kong Xiangxi, Huang Musong, Chen Shuren, Wang Shijie, Wu Dingchang, He Yingqin, Zhang Jia'ao, Chen Shaokuan, Liu Ruiheng, and Zhang Qun. Chairman: Chiang Kai-shek.

Matters for Discussion: Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Railways presented a proposal to reorganize the debt of the Daokou-Qinghua and Qinghua-Mengxian railways, along with a notification and a schedule of principal and interest repayments, requesting review and filing. Resolution: Passed and reported to the Central Political Conference. The President proposed that Ding Wenjiang, Director-General of the Academia Sinica, had devoted his life to promoting academic research, upholding integrity in mining, and making significant contributions to geology. He unfortunately died of coal poisoning while surveying mines in Hunan, sacrificing his life for the country, which is deeply regrettable. It is proposed that the Yuan submit a request to the National Government for a public commendation to honor his loyalty and encourage future generations. Resolution: Passed. Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries proposed the organization of the China Vegetable Oil Materials Factory Co., Ltd., with detailed plans and company articles of association, requesting a public decision. Resolution: Passed. Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries proposed, based on the principles approved in the conclusion of the Office for the Protection of Fisheries, a draft of measures for the Ministry's Fisheries Syndicate, requesting a public decision. Resolution: Passed.

Appointments and Dismissals: Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs requested submission to the National Government of a special appointment of Guo Taiqi as the plenipotentiary representative of our country for the revision of the Treaty of Friendship with Latvia. Resolution: Passed. Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs requested the dismissal of Zhu Changnian, the Minister to Sweden and concurrently Minister to Norway, pending further assignment, and requested the appointment of Wang Jingqi as the plenipotentiary Minister to Sweden and concurrently Minister to Norway. Resolution: Passed. Minister Jiang of the Ministry of Interior Affairs requested the appointment of Tang Bunian as a counselor of the Ministry. Resolution: Passed. Chairman Liu Xiang of the Sichuan Provincial Government requested the appointment of Li Hongyin as the Mayor of Chongqing. Resolution: Passed. (Central News Agency telegram, 12th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industries has drafted measures for organizing a Fisheries Syndicate, which have been passed by the Executive Yuan meeting. The contents are as follows: 1. The Ministry of Industries will improve fisheries by joining forces with various banks in Shanghai to organize a Fisheries Syndicate to handle the following matters: Promote the organization of fishermen's cooperatives; Provide loans for fisheries; Build new-style fishing vessels and lease them to fishermen. 2. The Fisheries Syndicate's office will be located at the Shanghai Fish Market. 3. Participating banks will appoint a representative to be responsible for managing the affairs of the Fisheries Syndicate. 4. The Ministry of Industries will send one supervisor to inspect the Fisheries Syndicate's business at any time. 5. The Fisheries Syndicate's capital will be divided into two types: fixed capital and circulating capital. The fixed capital will be invested by the Ministry of Industries starting from the 25th year at 200,000 yuan per year. The circulating capital will be determined annually by the Ministry of Industries and the participating banks based on the needs of the fisheries, but the total amount for the first year shall not be less than 800,000 yuan. 6. The fixed capital of the Fisheries Syndicate will accrue weekly interest at a rate of 6%, and the circulating capital will accrue weekly interest at a rate of 8%. 7. In addition to mortgage loans, all credit loans made by the Fisheries Syndicate must be guaranteed by cooperatives recognized by the Syndicate or the Shanghai Fish Market. 8. The Fisheries Syndicate's loan interest and income from fishing vessel rentals, after deducting interest on fixed and circulating capital, will all be used as reserve funds. 9. The Fisheries Syndicate's operating expenses must be kept to a minimum and approved by the Ministry of Industries, to be paid from the reserve fund. 10. If the Fisheries Syndicate has a surplus in its annual final accounts, dividends will be distributed according to the amount of fixed and circulating capital invested. If there is a loss, it may be covered by the reserve fund. If it is still insufficient, it may be supplemented by the interest on the fixed capital. If it is still insufficient, the Ministry of Industries may be requested to approve a reduction in the accumulated amount of the original fixed capital investment. 11. After the Fisheries Syndicate's annual final accounts are completed, the fixed capital should pay interest and dividends, which may be added to the amount of fixed capital with the approval of the Ministry of Industries. (Special dispatch, 12th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industries has decided to establish a Vegetable Oil Materials Factory, with a capital of 2,000,000 yuan, jointly operated by the government and private sector. The main factory will be located in Shanghai, with branch factories in major ports. The purpose is to improve quality and improve production and sales. The company's articles of association were passed by the Executive Yuan on the 12th, stipulating that the Ministry of Industries subscribe to 5,000 shares, totaling 500,000 yuan, and Sichuan, Hubei, Hunan, Zhejiang, and Guangxi each subscribe to 3,000 shares, totaling 1,500,000 yuan. The Ministry of Industries and the provincial governments may solicit private shares for half of their subscriptions. A board of directors consisting of 17 members will be established, with official shares represented by 8 directors, of whom 3 will be designated by the Ministry of Industries, and Sichuan, Hunan, Hubei, Zhejiang, and Guangxi provinces will each nominate one person to serve. The 9 private share directors will be elected by shareholders holding 60 or more shares. The directors will elect one person as chairman and one person as vice-chairman. Seven supervisors will be appointed, including one standing supervisor. One general manager and one or two deputy general managers will be appointed by the Ministry of Industries upon recommendation by the board of directors. Each factory will have one factory director, and if necessary, a deputy factory director may be added, who will be responsible for the affairs of each factory. (Special dispatch, 12th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways has negotiated with creditors on a reorganization plan for the deferred Daokou-Qinghua loan, Qinghua-Mengxian advance, and vehicle loan, and has submitted it to the Executive Yuan, which was approved at the Yuan meeting on the 12th. The original text of the plan is recorded below: A. 1905 Loan Bonds: From the 25th to the 27th year of the Republic, interest will be paid at a rate of 2.5% per year. If there is a surplus of Daokou-Qinghua funds after paying various expenses and loan payments, the rate will be increased to no more than 5%. Thereafter, interest will be paid at a rate of 5% per year. Principal: Starting from July of the 25th year of the Republic, it will be repaid in 27 years. Previously accumulated interest will be reduced by four-fifths, and the remaining one-fifth will be issued as interest-free notes, which will be repaid after the principal of the 27th-year loan is repaid. B. Qinghua-Mengxian advance and vehicle loan: Previously accumulated interest will be reduced to a simple annual interest rate of 3%, calculated up to the date of reorganization. The aforementioned simple interest, together with the principal, will no longer accrue interest thereafter and will be repaid in 12 years starting from July of the 25th year of the Republic. No interest will be paid on the aforementioned amount due if it is paid within six months. If it is not paid within six months, a simple annual interest rate of 4% will be paid. (Central News Agency telegram, 12th)

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan passed in principle the articles of association for the China Vegetable Oil Materials Factory Co., Ltd., which was planned by the Ministry of Industries, during its meeting on the 12th. The 20 articles of association include the following key points: The purpose of the factory is to improve the quality of vegetable oil materials, standardize standards, and improve all production and sales management matters. It is named the China Vegetable Oil Materials Factory. The factory will be jointly operated by the government and private sector and organized as a joint-stock company in accordance with the Company Law. The factory's main business is to act as an agent for storing and refining tung oil and to facilitate its transportation and sales. The scope of business includes the following: 1. Acting as an agent for the storage and refining of tung oil. 2. Acting as an agent for the storage and refining of other vegetable oils. 3. Acting as an agent for underwriting loans, remittance mortgages, reporting transportation and sales, and other matters that facilitate sales. 4. Refining lubricating oil materials. 5. Manufacturing oil paints and coatings. In order to concentrate and improve, regarding the storage, manufacturing, refining, and pressing of tung oil, after the Ministry of Industries submits it to the Executive Yuan for approval, no other organization with the same business is allowed in the country except for this factory. The company's headquarters will be located in Shanghai as the general office, and factories will be established in Shanghai, Hankou, Changsha, Changde, Wanxian, Chongqing, Hangzhou, Wenzhou, Wuzhou, and other places in order of business needs, subject to the resolution of the board of directors. The total capital is set at 2,000,000 yuan, divided into 20,000 shares. Half will be collected first, and the remainder will be paid in as necessary. The Ministry of Industries will subscribe to 5,000 shares, and the provincial governments of Sichuan, Hubei, Hunan, Zhejiang, and Guangxi will each subscribe to 30 shares. The Ministry of Industries and the provincial governments may solicit private shares for half of their subscriptions. If other oil-producing provinces are willing to subscribe to shares, the total amount of share capital may be increased as appropriate, or the shares subscribed by the Ministry of Industries may be preferentially transferred. The factory will have a board of directors consisting of 17 members, with official shares represented by 8 directors, of whom 3 will be designated by the Ministry of Industries, and the provincial governments of Sichuan, Hubei, Hunan, Zhejiang, and Guangxi will each designate one person to serve. The 9 private share directors will be elected by shareholders holding 60 or more shares. The directors will elect a chairman and a vice-chairman. The factory will have one or two general managers, who will be appointed by the Ministry of Industries upon recommendation by the board of directors, with a term of four years. Each factory will have one factory director, and if necessary, a deputy factory director may be added, who will be proposed by the general manager and appointed with the consent of the board of directors. The factory will have 7 supervisors, 3 of whom will be designated by official shares, and 4 of whom will be elected by shareholders holding 20 or more shares. The factory will have one standing supervisor, who will be elected by the supervisors. At the end of each year, a final settlement will be made. One-tenth of the net profit will be set aside as a statutory reserve fund. Commercial shares will be paid 8% interest, and official shares will be paid 6% interest. If there is still a surplus, it will be used as a shareholder dividend and employee bonus. The allocation amount will be resolved and distributed by the board of directors. (Central News Agency telegram, 12th)

Yangtze River Water Rises in the Upper Reaches; Six Provinces and Cities to Hold Flood Prevention Conference 10

(Nanjing) Due to continuous rain in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the water level is gradually rising, especially in the Xiang River, where the situation is becoming increasingly serious. A reporter recently visited Fu Rulin to inquire about flood prevention preparations. According to him, the Water Resources Commission is paying close attention to the sudden increase in the river level. In addition to reinforcing and consolidating the river embankments last year, the Commission has also sent letters to various provincial governments, ordering the responsible authorities to make urgent preparations in accordance with the previously promulgated flood prevention measures. To properly plan flood prevention, a Yangtze River Flood Prevention Conference for six provinces and cities will be held on the 27th. The Construction Department heads of the five provinces and the Director of the Public Works Bureau of Nanjing City have been telegraphed to attend the meeting in Nanjing to discuss and coordinate actions. (Central News Agency telegram, 12th)

Conference of Senior Local Administrative Personnel to Discuss Civil Affairs and Education Proposals; Deliberations on Public Security Matters Today; Closing Ceremony This Afternoon 11

(Nanjing) At the Conference of Senior Local Administrative Personnel, the general assembly on the 12th discussed civil affairs proposals in the morning, chaired by Jiang Zuobin. After the meeting, Kong Xiangxi hosted a banquet for all attendees. In the afternoon, the meeting continued to discuss education proposals, chaired by Wang Shijie, and adjourned at 5:00 PM. Wang Shijie, Weng Wenhao, and Jiang Tingfu hosted a banquet for all attendees, which ended at 7:00 PM. The general assembly will continue on the 13th to discuss public security proposals, chaired by He Yingqin. After discussions, the closing ceremony will be held in the afternoon.

The deliberation on civil affairs proposals resulted in six decided solutions: The joint office of the provincial government should still be thoroughly implemented to achieve the expected goals. Some joint offices have increased cumbersome paperwork, but the reason is not the joint office itself, but the failure to thoroughly integrate. After the joint office in Hubei, personnel and expenses have been reduced, and efficiency has increased compared to before. The relationship between the departments and the provincial government is similar to that between the departments of the central government. The commissioner system, if used properly, can assist the provincial government in implementing policies and supervising the actual implementation of policies in various counties. However, the commissioner's office should be further strengthened as part of the provincial government, and its authority should be further defined. The principle of the county government abolishing bureaus and changing them to sections is very good. It can reduce administrative expenses and avoid administrative constraints. However, it still depends on the complexity of the work, the amount of expenses, and the local conditions. For education and construction, if financial resources are sufficient, it is still appropriate to set up two separate sections. Establishing branch offices in counties can assist the county government in implementing policies and avoid the drawbacks of overly large county areas and difficult governance. However, the expenses and personnel of the district offices must be properly planned in advance. Actively promote land policies, especially paying attention to land surveys. The reporting is only slightly less expensive than the land survey, and it is not a fundamental solution. The central government should organize large-scale triangulation and aerial surveys as soon as possible to establish the foundation of land administration. Building warehouses and accumulating grain is rarely implemented in various places. Efforts should be made to improve this practice, and it should not be adhered to rigidly. Pay attention to how to use the accumulated grain to stabilize grain prices, circulate finance, and regulate the rural economy.

The deliberation on education basic proposals resulted in four items: Extending compulsory education and increasing funding: (A) Regarding funding: (1) A portion of the original funding of each county and city, if it is deemed to be similar to miscellaneous taxes, should still be effectively compensated in accordance with the order before it can be handled. (2) Designate one or more types from the various taxes of the central government or provinces (such as salt tax, deed tax, business tax, slaughter tax, etc.), or attach a percentage to a certain tax, and collect a sufficient amount to be used exclusively for compulsory education funding. (3) If difficulties arise during the implementation of Article 5, Section 2, and Section 5 of the Provisional Measures for Raising Compulsory Education Funds in Various Provinces and Cities issued by the Executive Yuan, the central government should provide more specific regulations to facilitate implementation. (4) Add a clause to the Provisional Measures for Raising Compulsory Education Funds in Various Provinces and Cities, allowing elementary school districts to solicit donations from households in the district based on their wealth. (5) A portion of the security expenses reduced by each province and the surplus from the reorganization of land taxes should be used as funding. (6) The central government is requested to double the compulsory education subsidy funding in the 25th fiscal year and instruct the provinces and cities to do the same. (B) Regarding teachers: (1) Teacher training is considered a major task for promoting compulsory education in the next year. (2) When training teachers, the departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities should set up temporary classes to train unemployed graduates of secondary schools and above and submit a request to use the central compulsory education funding. Improving productive education: (A) Each province's vocational education funding must be increased to reach the proportion set by the Ministry, and the central government is requested to allocate considerable funding in the 25th fiscal year to subsidize excellent vocational schools. (B) In accordance with the principle of cooperation between construction and education, the relevant central government agencies should formulate concrete measures at any time. (C) Each province's technical personnel training class should be managed by the Department of Education. (D) Special attention should be paid to the labor science of primary and secondary schools. Implementing mass education: (A) Regarding mass schools and mass training: (1) Flexibility should be reserved in the measures for phasing, to suit the actual situation of the province. It is said that this is determined by the central government and supplemented by the local government. (2) Unified measures should be formulated for mass education and mass training, such as civil soldiers, national military training, youth service, women's service, etc., and there should be close contact. (3) Rural elementary schools and short-term elementary schools should run mass training classes if they cannot implement the two-part system. (4) The central government should provide special funding to subsidize the funding for training teachers in mass schools. (B) Regarding broadcasting and film education, they should be implemented effectively in accordance with the original measures and attention should be paid to improving teaching materials and technology. Actively promote school and mass health education to train national physique: (A) The amount of health education funding allocated by each province and city should be flexible and determined by the Ministry. (B) In addition to the central government organizing health teacher training, the Department of Health is requested to assist each province and city in organizing it by region.

At the general assembly on the morning of the 13th, a public security plan was decided. The scope of discussion included cases such as the promotion of the baojia system, the police system, and the rise and fall of security teams. After the discussions, the closing ceremony was announced. (Central News Agency telegram, 12th)

(Nanjing) At the general assembly on the morning of the 12th of the Conference of Senior Local Administrative Personnel, the proposals of the civil affairs group were fully discussed. In the afternoon, the general assembly continued to discuss the proposals of the education group. The general assembly continued on the morning of the 13th to discuss the proposals of the public security group, and the closing ceremony was held in the afternoon. (Special dispatch, 12th)

(Nanjing) Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi returned to Nanjing on the morning of the 12th to attend the Executive Yuan meeting, where he reported on financial issues to President Chiang. Kong hosted a luncheon for all attendees of the administrative personnel meeting at the Lihzhi Society. In the evening, he hosted a banquet for the ministers of the foreign affairs and railways departments at his private residence. (Special dispatch, 12th)

League of Nations Council Decides to Maintain Sanctions Against Italy: Full Dispute to be Discussed in Mid-June: Italian Representative Announces Immediate Departure from Geneva 27

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council, continuing its meeting at 5 p.m. today, passed a resolution stipulating that the Italian-Ethiopian dispute should be discussed at an extraordinary meeting to be convened on June 15, and that sanctions against Italy should be maintained from now until then. (Havas, 12th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council held an important meeting today and, after rejecting the strong protests of Italian representative Aloisi, resolved to retain the Abyssinian issue on the Council's agenda, which is tantamount to ruling that Abyssinia is still a member state of the League of Nations and should be protected by the League. After the Spanish and Danish representatives spoke against the Italian representative's proposal to remove the Italian-Ethiopian dispute from the agenda, the proposal was put to a vote. The representatives present unanimously advocated retaining the original agenda. Italy, as the creator of the dispute, its vote was not counted. After the vote was taken, the Italian chief representative, Aloisi, led members of the Italian delegation out of the meeting to express their opposition to the Council's actions and to the presence of Ethiopian representative Mariam. Aloisi declared that he could not allow the so-called Abyssinian representative to attend the meeting, and that only Italians now enjoyed the rights of Abyssinia, so any discussion of the so-called dispute was invalid, and he would not participate in this discussion. Thereupon, the Ethiopian representative Mariam rose to speak a few words on the status of Abyssinia. The major Italian-Ethiopian dispute will be discussed at the Council's public meeting tomorrow. It is heard that a resolution will be proposed tomorrow to postpone the issue to an extraordinary meeting around June 15. (Reuters, 11th)

(Geneva) The representatives of the Council member states held a meeting last night to discuss a resolution stating that the Italian-Ethiopian dispute should be postponed for further discussion until the Council's extraordinary meeting on June 15, and that the sanctions against Italy should continue to be implemented before June 15. The issue of the sovereignty of the Ethiopian emperor will not be raised for discussion at that time. (Havas, 12th)

(Geneva) Italian representative Aloisi recently notified League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol that the delegation has been instructed by the government to leave Geneva today. The intention behind Italy's move is not yet known. (Havas, 12th)

League of Nations Council Meeting: Italy and Ethiopia Irreconcilable: Representatives of the Two Countries Play a Game of Hide-and-Seek 29

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council held a closed-door meeting at 5:45 p.m. British Foreign Secretary Eden chaired the meeting. The Ethiopian representative, Wald, had already entered the chamber and taken his seat before the meeting began, which shows that the Council members have always recognized Abyssinia as a member state. Italian Chief Representative Aloisi then arrived and, upon seeing Wald in his seat, immediately made a long-distance call to Rome for instructions. Shortly thereafter, the Council announced that the meeting would begin. The agenda was first put forward for discussion. Chairman Eden then raised the Italian-Ethiopian issue and formally invited Wald to attend the meeting. Thereupon, Aloisi stood up and declared, "The state of Abyssinia no longer exists. The sovereignty of that country belongs to Italy. As the Italian representative cannot tolerate the presence of the so-called Abyssinian representative, any discussion on the Italian-Ethiopian issue is meaningless. I must therefore refuse to participate in the discussion." After speaking, he left the meeting. After Aloisi left the meeting, the Chairman declared that the issue at hand was whether or not to include the Italian-Ethiopian issue on the agenda, and that he thought it was appropriate to include it. Spain's Madariaga and Denmark's representative Menchu also expressed their support. The representatives of the Council member states then held a meeting at the invitation of British Foreign Secretary Eden in the evening, and decided that the Italian-Ethiopian issue should be announced as postponed for discussion at the next meeting, but the date of the meeting was not set. An extraordinary meeting of the Council is scheduled to be convened on June 15 to discuss the Italian-Ethiopian issue and the Locarno Treaty. (Havas, 11th)

(Geneva) After Italian representative Aloisi left the meeting, the Council immediately held a public meeting to discuss the other items on the agenda. At this time, Ethiopian representative Wald had left the meeting, and Aloisi had quietly returned to his seat. The Council then voted to pass several reports, one of which was drafted by Aloisi. It was then announced that the meeting would be adjourned, and the date for the resumption of the meeting was not decided. It is generally believed that the Council may reconvene on Wednesday (the 13th), at which time it will disregard the opposition of the Italian representative and resume discussion of the Italian-Ethiopian issue. Ethiopian representative Wald may give a speech at the Council on that day, and then the Council will formally announce that this issue will be postponed for discussion until June. People from the Italian delegation recently issued a statement saying that Aloisi was still present when the Council held its public meeting, which shows that his intention in leaving the meeting was only to oppose the presence of the Ethiopian representative. Other delegations said that although Italy claimed that the Abyssinian issue was no longer relevant to the League of Nations, the Council should still put it forward for discussion, which shows that the position adopted by Italy has been unanimously rejected by the Council, and its attitude is very firm, which is worthy of attention. (Havas, 11th)

It must be known that the Abyssinian people have not surrendered, and the vast land west of our capital is still intact, free and independent, as always. We still want to rely on this, and follow the example of other nations, with the spirit of enduring hardship and humiliation, to drive the aggressors out of the country," and so on. (Havas, 11th)

Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü Aras has confirmed this and stated that the relevant countries have, in principle, agreed with his country's proposals. The economic and commercial provisions contained in the Lausanne Treaty will not be amended. The guarantor nations – Britain, France, Italy, and Japan – along with the other four signatory nations, namely Greece, Yugoslavia, Romania, and Bulgaria, will participate in the meeting. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) On April 11th, the Turkish government sent a note to the signatory nations of the Lausanne Treaty, namely Britain, France, Italy, Japan, Romania, Yugoslavia, Greece, and Bulgaria, requesting an amendment to the armament provisions concerning the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits. Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü Aras, who is here to attend the regular session of the League of Nations Council, will present the request to the representatives of the Lausanne Treaty signatory nations, asking for a meeting to be held in Montreux, Switzerland, on June 25th to discuss the amendment issue. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Successful North Atlantic Flight: "Hindenburg" Returns Home, Passing Over New York's Skyscrapers; Crowds Stop and Look Up, Cheering Loudly 40

Lakehurst, New Jersey, USA: The German airship "Hindenburg," which arrived here on the 8th of this month from the Friedrichshafen airfield in Germany, taking a total of 62 hours, thus setting a new speed record, departed from here at 3:27 AM this morning to fly back to Germany. The ship's captain, Dr. Eckener, also gave a speech before departure, hoping to arrive on the European Atlantic coast within 46 hours. The ship is carrying 47 passengers and 2.57 tons of mail and cargo. It flew over Manhattan Island in New York, passing skyscrapers. The lights of the entire ship were brilliantly lit, and it was extremely beautiful. The crowds on the ground stopped and looked up, cheering loudly. After flying over New York, the ship headed straight for the coast, flying over the Atlantic Ocean, taking advantage of the wind. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Lakehurst, New Jersey: The German airship "Hindenburg" has now departed from its base in Friedrichshafen, Germany, crossed the North Atlantic, and arrived in the United States in 60 hours and 30 minutes, setting a new record for airships. Today, it has departed from here to fly back to its German base. The airship, which was recently built, has already successfully completed three remarkable flights: two across the South Atlantic between Germany and Brazil, and one across the Atlantic. After arriving in Germany, this will be its fourth flight. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Japanese Army Minister Advocates Strengthening Troops Stationed in Manchuria to Defend Against Russia; Seeks Unified Command for Troops Stationed in North China; Navy Seeks Parity with Britain and the United States 41

(Tokyo) According to reliable sources, Army Minister Terauchi declared in a closed session of the Diet today that since the Soviet Union first proposed concluding a non-aggression pact, relations between Japan and Russia have not only failed to improve but have worsened. The overall situation is now particularly tense. The Soviet Union has built numerous fortresses along the border between Manchuria and Mongolia. From the Japanese perspective, this move is indeed of an aggressive nature. The Soviet Union has not abandoned its policy of "Bolshevizing" the world. According to reliable reports, the Soviet Union's troops stationed in the Far East already exceed 200,000 and may increase to 300,000 in the future. In addition, the port of Vladivostok is home to 50 submarines and air squadrons capable of attacking Japanese cities. Outer Mongolia is now completely under Soviet protection, which is enough to surround "Manchukuo." This situation forces Japan to station a large army in Manchuria. The military has so far opposed concluding a non-aggression pact with the Soviet Union, viewing the Soviet Union's proposal as worthless. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Tokyo) The Asahi Shimbun today reported that Navy Minister Nagano stated at a closed-door Diet meeting discussing the budget that the Japanese Navy wants to have a strength comparable to the most powerful naval country that could attack Japan. In view of the current situation, it is absolutely necessary for Japan to implement appropriate defensive preparations, such as naval bases. Between 1931 and 1933, the Japanese Navy built an average of 22,000 tons of warships each year, while Britain averaged 33,000 tons and the United States 48,000 tons. The average cost per ton of capital ship is approximately between 2,500 and 3,000 yuan. The Navy Minister also said that the time for achieving equality with Britain and the United States has not yet been determined. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Tokyo) The gist of the answers given by the Army and Navy Ministers at today's closed-door meeting regarding Japan's national defense plan at 10:00 AM are as follows:

Navy Minister Nagano: Japan's operational strategy is passive. If Japan's strength is equal to that of its opponent, then the opponent can come and attack Japan, and Japan can also go and attack. However, Japan's policy is not to attack, but to maintain a military force that is insufficient to attack but sufficient to defend. Under this policy, we demand that we maintain a force in the waters near Japan that is equal to the strength that the world's largest naval power can send there. It is not yet known how much it will cost to build ships after the treaties expire, but generally speaking, the cost will not be much different from the cost during the treaty period. From 1931 to 1935, the annual tonnage of ships built by various countries was as follows: Japan 22,000 tons, Britain 33,000 tons, and the United States 48,000 tons. The cost of building a capital ship is 2,500 to 3,000 yuan per ton.

Army Minister Terauchi: People say that because the Soviet Union has advocated the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty, it will definitely not launch a sudden attack. However, this was the case when the Soviet Union was implementing its Five-Year Plan. The facts today are completely different. According to some people, the Soviet Union's transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway proves that it has abandoned its Far Eastern policy. However, the Soviet Union transferred the Chinese Eastern Railway because it saw its value; it was not an abandonment of its Far Eastern policy. The Soviet Union is rushing to build military facilities along its vast borders, calling it defensive rather than offensive. However, from a military point of view, it is entirely an offensive setup. The Soviet Union has not abandoned its policy of socialism and world communization. It is now using the Siberian Railway as a center to send troops to the Far East, the number of which has reached more than 200,000 and may reach 300,000 in the future. This is the same as the strength of the Russian army in the Battle of the Sha River during the Russo-Japanese War. Vladivostok now has 50 submarines and an air squadron capable of attacking the capital of Japan. It has also placed Outer Mongolia under its control, surrounding "Manchukuo." Because the facts are as described above, Japan must have a necessary force stationed in Manchuria. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 12th)

(Tokyo) A closed-door meeting of the House of Representatives was held on the 11th. The following is a summary of the questions and answers between the two ministers of the military and the members of the committee:

Tegami Koujirou (Minseito): The United States has no intention of going to war with Japan over the China issue. From a broader perspective, how about Japan proposing to the United States to stop the naval arms race?

Foreign Minister Arita: It is not yet known how the United States views Japan's attitude towards China and how it will respond to Japan's proposal. However, it is quite difficult to determine the extent to which the United States will accept Japan's proposal.

Ashida Hitoshi (Seiyukai): Since the treaties restricting armaments will expire, Japan can newly implement defenses within its territory. Has the government considered the cost?

Navy Minister Nagano: It is not yet known whether such a necessity will arise in the future, but it has not been planned for at present.

After an exchange between Ashida and Foreign Minister Arita regarding the state of Japanese goods being imported into North China, he said, "Regarding the issue of warship types, what are the advantages and disadvantages of the Italian and Chinese [strategies of] a small number of large ships versus a large number of small ships?"

Navy Minister Nagano: This is a question that needs to be researched and experimented with. However, we intend to avoid discussing the issue of warship types.

Okuchi Kihachi (Seiyukai): What is the estimated naval expenditure for 1935 to 1937?

Navy Minister Nagano: The figures are not yet known. Matsumoto Tadao (Minseito): Japan proposed equal naval strength for Britain, Japan, and the United States at the London Conference. At that time, did the naval authorities consider concretely realizing this equality within a few years?

Navy Minister Nagano: Because Britain and the United States did not accept Japan's proposal, the number of years has not been determined.

Miyawaki Nagakichi (Seiyukai): It is said that the number of armaments prepared by the Soviet Union in the Far East is exaggerated compared to the actual number. Is this true?

Army Minister Terauchi: The figures we have obtained are reports from reliable sources and are not exaggerated.

Hazeta Akira (Neutral): Will future naval expenditures increase to an alarming level?

Navy Minister Nagano: They will not increase to an alarming level. In my opinion, the expenditure will be roughly the same as the expenditure during the treaty era, with no major difference.

Hazeta Akira: What will future army expenditures be?

Army Minister Terauchi: It is not convenient to say.

Kamei Kanichiro: What about the secret agreement between the Chinese government and the Soviet Union?

Army Minister Terauchi: I don't know.

Kamei and Navy Minister Nagano asked questions about shipbuilding plans and defense issues. Next, Sakurai Hyogorou (Minseito) said that the Soviet Union's proposal to Japan to conclude a non-aggression treaty is a reality.

Army Minister Terauchi: We do not consider the Soviet Union's proposal for a non-aggression treaty to be of value. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 12th)

Army Minister's Answers in the Diet

(London) At today's meeting of the House of Commons, Conservative MP Knox mentioned the mutual assistance agreement between the Soviet Union and Outer Mongolia and asked to what extent Outer Mongolia had become an independent country. Clearing Out Communist Bandits in Shanxi Province: Authorities Hasten Post-Disaster Recovery, Dispatching Large Forces Across the River to Pursue and Suppress, and Issuing Telegrams to Counties to Comfort the People 54

Taiyuan Correspondence: The communist bandits disturbing Shanxi, after being severely suppressed and routed, the remaining remnants have fled back towards northern Shaanxi. As of now, Shanxi province has been completely cleared. The counties that were troubled by the bandits are still engaged in cleansing operations. Investigations reveal that the communist bandits' incursion into Shanxi lasted nearly three months, disturbing more than thirty counties. Everywhere they went, the local losses were such that almost all houses were emptied. In some places, only scorched earth remained, uninhabitable. According to those returning from inspections at the front lines, although the communist bandits' strength has suffered greatly, the amount of wealth and food they looted was substantial. If the National Army does not thoroughly suppress them in their old nest in northern Shaanxi, the future hidden dangers are truly unpredictable. It is said that the Xue family, a wealthy family in Xinjiang, alone was robbed of 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. Some say the actual amount was even greater. Several families in Hongdong and Linfen counties were also robbed, and the amount of losses was even greater. Currently, the authorities are actively coordinating military operations to suppress the bandits, ordering forces to cross the river and pursue them. In addition to the central government's troops entering Shanxi, which will be largely deployed, the Shanxi army has also decided to dispatch its elite forces to advance westward. The railway between Pingyao and Fenyang is being rushed to completion, with a deadline of ten days. After the large army in southern Shanxi moves north along the Tongpu Railway, it will then be transferred westward along that railway.

It is reported that the Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters is not only urgently drafting the second phase of military plans, but also, together with the provincial government, is rapidly planning for local post-disaster recovery. Yan Xishan has specifically telegraphed the counties affected by the bandits, ordering them to actively handle the situation. The original telegram is recorded below: "To all armies, heads of all anti-communist defense corps, county magistrates, and heads of all advocacy groups: During this communist bandit incursion into Shanxi, more than 30,000 people crossed the river in succession. This headquarters promptly dispatched troops from all directions and requested the central government to send large forces to Shanxi to assist in suppressing them in dozens of battles, large and small. According to statistics, the number of bandits killed, wounded, captured, and surrendered is more than half. Later, with the completion of our blockhouse lines, the bandits were encircled between Xixian, Yonghe, and Daning, and repeatedly subjected to severe attacks. The bandits were exhausted and, taking advantage of the night, led their remnants from Qingshui Pass and Yujiazui back to northern Shaanxi. There are no more bandit traces in our province. Investigations reveal that the bandits disturbed more than thirty counties in Shanxi, harassing our localities, poisoning our people, and causing countless losses, both public and private. As the director, I am responsible for inadequate coordination, failing to prevent their arrival and failing to prevent their westward escape. Reflecting on my duties, I feel deeply indebted. In addition to informing the central government for punishment, all counties affected by the bandits should quickly comfort the people, expedite post-disaster recovery, eliminate the remaining evils, and intensify political work to stabilize the people's livelihoods and pacify the localities. Director Yan Geng (8th) stamped at noon." (May 9th)

Chairman Chiang Inspects Hunan Province, Overview of Hunan's Administration, He Jian Begins Organizing the Pacification Headquarters 55

Changsha Correspondence: The fiscal revenue and expenditure for Hunan Province in the 25th year of the Republic (1936) have been compiled and completed by the provincial government. The recurring revenue is estimated at 10,466,625 yuan, and the temporary revenue is 5,256,877 yuan, totaling 15,724,502 yuan. After offsetting expenditures, this is a decrease of over 868,000 yuan compared to the 24th year of the Republic (1935). Recently, since the communist bandits in the province have been cleared out, the province is now fully engaged in construction projects. The methods for suppressing communist bandits were uniquely created by Hunan. For example, the construction of blockhouses was designed by He Jian in Hunan during the suppression of communists in the 19th year of the Republic (1930). Furthermore, the organizational laws for the local militia and volunteer army were traditional methods since Zuo Zongtang, and He Jian has carried them forward. After Jiangxi province imitated and adopted Hunan's tactics for suppressing bandits, it was able to escape the communist bandits' troubles. Last year, there were many complicated troop deployments entering Hunan from various directions, and orders were inconsistent. Later, Chairman Chiang gave He Jian full authority, and he was able to completely clear out the communist bandits in one to two months. Now that the military affairs have come to an end, he is beginning to organize the Changsha Pacification Headquarters. Chairman Chiang especially flew to Changsha from Guizhou on the 27th of last month to personally instruct He Jian on strategies and advise the people of all circles in Hunan to work diligently under the guidance of Chairman He. He also pointed out that Hunan province is the central region for national salvation. After Chairman Chiang's inspection and commendation of the people of Hunan, their work has progressed even further. Investigations reveal that the Guangdong-Hankou Railway was fully connected on April 28th. For transportation purposes, the railway bureau has been changed to set up offices at both ends for convenience. It is planned to hold a full line opening ceremony on Double Tenth Day (October 10th). Furthermore, the Hunan-Guizhou highway has been 80% completed, and the Hunan-Sichuan highway has been 15% completed, with construction being rushed day and night, with the number of workers increased to over 30,000. Recently, Secretary-General Weng Wenhao of the Executive Yuan visited Hunan and inspected various construction projects, expressing great satisfaction and promising to allocate funds for subsidies after returning to the capital. The Hunan Provincial Government, in consideration of the suffering of the people in the bandit areas, has specially exempted Liuyang County from the full year of unpaid land tax for the 20th and 21st years of the Republic (1931 and 1932). There is also the initiative to designate Hengshan County as an experimental model county. Furthermore, Chairman He has issued an order to all county Confucius temples, strictly prohibiting military troops from being stationed there. A military-civilian equestrian competition will be held in Changsha on the 10th of this month, and plans are being made to organize a Chinese orchestra to promote proper recreational interests among the people. At the same time, the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee has added a branch office for persuasion and abstinence in the provincial capital, ordering all counties to sign anti-smoking pledges to create a healthy population in the province and strengthen national power. Separately, Chairman He has drafted various suggestions for good governance and submitted them to Chairman Chiang for reference, and it is said that they have received high praise. (10th)

Guangdong Province: Luofu Scenic Spot, Zoned for Development and Reclamation, Wasteland Leased to People for Cultivation, Annual Rent of Two Jiao Per Mu, Exempted for Three Years 56

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong provincial authorities regard Mount Luofu as a famous scenic spot in the province. In order to develop the mountain and preserve historical sites, it was previously decided to transform it into a summer resort and build a park. Now, the Department of Construction believes that in addition to the designated agricultural and forestry areas and residential areas, there is still much wasteland on the mountain. It is urgent to designate sections of land as special reclamation areas and attract people to lease and cultivate them, so that barren land can be transformed into fertile land. Therefore, it has drafted regulations for leasing land in the area and submitted them to the provincial government for inspection and approval. The case was submitted yesterday to the 485th Provincial Affairs Meeting for modification and approval. The original proposal and the land distribution regulations are recorded below:

"Case: Regarding the case of developing Mount Luofu as a summer resort, the department previously drafted a plan, regulations, and budget, which were submitted to the government for approval and implementation. Now, investigations reveal that in addition to the designated agricultural and forestry areas and residential areas, there is still much wasteland on the mountain. It is urgent to designate sections of land as special reclamation areas and attract people to lease and cultivate them, so that barren land can be transformed into fertile land, and desolate areas can become prosperous. Not only will tourists become more interested, but nearby farmers will also be able to live and work in peace. This will provide some assistance in relieving rural areas. Now, with reference to the Mount Luofu Park Land Rental Regulations, we have tentatively prepared a copy of the Mount Luofu Special Reclamation Area Land Lease Regulations and submitted it to the meeting. We believe that this is appropriate and respectfully await your decision." Attached is a copy of the Mount Luofu Special Reclamation Area Land Lease Regulations: Article 1: Various sections within the scope of Mount Luofu Park, in addition to the designated residential areas and agricultural and forestry areas, will also designate several sections as special reclamation areas, allowing people of the Republic of China to consult the sectional maps from the management office, select sections of land, and pay rent according to the regulations. Article 2: After the land lessee selects the leased land section at the management office, they shall immediately receive a land lease certificate. Article 3: The annual rent for each mu of special reclamation area is two jiao, exempted for three years. Article 4: The special reclamation area is limited to sixty years, and the lease can be renewed upon expiration. Article 5: The land lease certificate is valid for one year. If the land lessee does not start cultivation after the expiration, it will be invalidated, and the management office may approve another person to lease it. Article 6: The official rent is one yuan per certificate, and the survey fee is three yuan. A replacement for lost certificates will be charged half price. Article 7: If there are any matters not stipulated in these regulations, they shall be handled in accordance with the Mount Luofu Park Land Rental Regulations. Article 8: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of submission to the provincial government for approval.

Guangdong Silk Implementation Area: Cooperative Enterprise Progresses, Silk Implementation Headquarters Established in Shunde, Agricultural Bank Loans Assist Development 57

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong provincial authorities have paid great attention to the improvement of the silk industry in recent years. The Department of Construction previously established a silk implementation headquarters in Daliang, Shunde County, and implementation areas in Huanglian and other places. The area is actively engaged in the improvement of the silk industry. It also pays great attention to silk by-products. Over the years, there have been significant results. The director of the area, Liao Chongzhen, is now assisting farmers in organizing various silk cooperatives, using cooperative organizations to improve the economic situation of silk farmers. He first organized a silk weaving cooperative in Lun Jiao and Shi Fen, specializing in weaving improved products and handling transportation and sales. Recently, in Le Liu, Huang Lian implementation area, the organization of the improved cocoon silk weaving cooperative, specializing in the business of weaving improved cocoon silk, is progressing and developing. Yesterday, the mulberry leaf purchasing cooperative for silk farmers was established in Le Liu, handling the purchase of mulberry leaves and lending them to poor farmers for silkworm rearing. Recently, there has been the organization of the silk floss production cooperative in Huanglian. Various cooperatives are guided by personnel dispatched by the Shunde Cooperative Enterprise Guidance Office. The Agricultural Bank is also very supportive and provides loans to assist the development of various cooperatives. (8th)

Jiangxi Province: Specialty Products Exhibition Held, Ceramics are the Most Numerous, The Rest are Various Agricultural Products 58

Nanchang Correspondence: For the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Specialty Products Exhibition, the two provinces have first pre-exhibited the collected specialty products in their own provinces, and then exchanged exhibitions for mutual promotion and sales. In the Jiangxi pre-exhibition, except for the ceramics concentrated in Jingdezhen manufacturers, the remaining items such as summer cloth, paper (fine and coarse), rice, tobacco leaves, tea leaves, shiitake mushrooms, tungsten ore, and coal were not concentrated in one place, so the scheduled opening date was delayed until the 8th. The venue is located in the former Xingying, now the Provincial Library. At 9:00 a.m., people from all walks of life and various agencies gathered in front of the library and the Shou Lequn Cinema for the opening ceremony. Over a thousand people, including Miao Peicheng, attended. The ceremony was chaired by Li Dezhao, Director of the Department of Construction, who gave a report on the significance of the meeting, stating that less than fifty of the eighty-three counties in the province had sent in specialty products, partly due to the lack of knowledge of business among the industrial and commercial sectors, and partly due to the county magistrates' perfunctory attitude, not knowing that developing specialty products is to promote the province's economy. Miao Peicheng and Yu Renqian, a representative from Zhejiang Province, then delivered speeches. After the ceremony, Director Li led the guests to visit the venue. The first exhibition hall is located in the Provincial Library. The first thing that catches the eye are the agricultural products from various regions, such as rice, beans, fruits, Guangfeng's tobacco leaves, Xiushui's tea, and famous local foods. Then there is the tungsten ore, which accounts for 60% of the world's production, and the nationally famous Pingxiang coal, as well as copper, iron, tin, and other minerals from various regions. There is also the Wanzai summer cloth, which is sold throughout the country and Southeast Asia, with many exquisite pieces. As for paper, before the import of foreign paper, Lian Shi, Mao Bian, and other papers had an annual output value of several million yuan, and many were collected. Among the woodenware, the famous camphor wood chests have many styles. The second exhibition hall is entirely dedicated to ceramics, with a wide variety of items. Various antique porcelains are the most valuable, such as the Yongzheng Wanhua Taibai Zun, priced at 5,000 yuan, and the Qianlong Wanhua Dong Hao landscape, priced at 3,000 yuan. Other works by the Four Great Masters, such as Wang Yeting, are also brilliantly displayed. It is said that after the closing ceremony, all the specialty products will be transported to Zhejiang Province for exhibition. (8th)

Songjiang: Punan Bandit Leader Arrested and Escorted to Songjiang 59

Last year, during the Double Tenth Day incident where a Shanghai-Chouzhou highway joint transport bus was robbed by bandits on horseback in the area of Lao Yanggong Temple north of Jinshanwei, the Provincial Security Command repeatedly ordered strict pursuit. Later, after the capture of the principal offenders Zhang Xiaobao and others, they confessed that Li Jinxiang was the ringleader. Immediate secret arrests were repeatedly decided, but the bandit leader was hiding in Shanghai and was never found. Recently, bandit cases have occurred frequently in various parts of Punan, and most of them were committed by Li Jinxiang's men. This time, Zhao Zanchen, the commander of the 12th Security Brigade, was ordered to suppress the bandits, believing that arresting the ringleader was necessary to warn the rest. According to confidential reports, the bandit leader was hiding in the Lan Ni Du area of Pudong. Commander Zhao hired a car to Shanghai at 3:00 a.m. on the 12th and arrived directly at the destination at dawn, arresting the bandit leader Li Jinxiang and his concubine Yu Xiaomei together. They then hired a car to escort them back to the team, and are currently under interrogation.

Suzhou: Student Sues Principal, Verdict Given 60

Cheng Wangjichang, principal of Suzhou Anding Middle School, was previously sued in the local court by over ten graduates of the school, including Xu Guoyuan, who hired lawyers Zhou Yuyong and Zhang Yu to file the suit. Unsuccessful Debt Collection Leads to Murder 61

In Beitang Village, about three miles from Xietang Town in Su Township, a villager named He Asan owed a neighbor named Dai Tuquan 1,000 cash. The day before yesterday, Dai Tuquan suddenly demanded the 1,000 cash debt from He Asan. Because He did not repay, Dai angrily beat He. At that time, the villagers persuaded them to disperse. Unexpectedly, less than two hours later, He Asan died from his injuries. The villagers, recognizing that it involved a matter of life and death, immediately sent the murderer Dai Tuquan to the 6th Sub-Bureau of the local public security office for interrogation, and at the same time reported it to the Procuratorate of the Local Court. On the 12th, Prosecutor Lü led officials to the village for inspection, confirming that the death was due to injuries. He immediately ordered the family to prepare the coffin and burial, and the Public Security Sub-Bureau transferred Dai Tuquan to the General Bureau and sent him to the court for interrogation.

Expansion of Sit-Down Strike in Foundry Factories 63

The six foundry factories, including Xicheng, Longchang, Huacheng, Guangqin, Xiangtai, and Sanxin, located by Huinong Bridge in the county, laid off workers to save expenses, causing a sit-down strike. It is learned that there are a total of eighteen foundry factories and over eighty machine factories in the county, with as many as two thousand workers. In the past, a foundry workers' union was established, but it was disbanded following the order to disband the General Labor Union. Recently, the county party headquarters has been actively restoring the General Labor Union, so the workers in the industry unanimously requested the factory to assist in restoring the union. At that time, the factory did not express any opinion, resulting in the labor unrest. The Foundry Industry Guild, because the workers' will was firm and mediation was ineffective, the situation was serious, so it convened representatives of capital and relevant parties to discuss countermeasures. It was decided that official letters would be sent to the County Chamber of Commerce, and then to the County Party Headquarters and County Government, requesting that they uphold justice and mediate according to law. Yesterday morning (12th), all the workers of the county unanimously went on strike. Although some workers continued their normal work, they were connected to the foundry factories. If the foundry workers do not resume work, the machine factories will inevitably be forced to shut down. It is heard that the authorities are trying to resolve the situation, but because no representatives from the workers have come forward to negotiate, a stalemate has formed, the situation has expanded and is beyond control, and it is difficult to resolve in the shortest time.

Detective Squad Captures Four Notorious Robbers 64

The home of Chen Xiangchun, a resident of Chen Lane west of Xiao Zhangjia Bridge outside the South Gate in the Second District, was broken into by more than ten robbers around 1:00 a.m. on December 28th of last year. They robbed a box cannon with number 331510, eight bullets, a rifle with number 1026, eight bullets, a white Lang Lin pistol with number 68358, six bullets, 117 yuan in legal tender, as well as gold jewelry, copper coins, clothing, etc., causing significant losses. The victim reported the case to the County Bureau for investigation. The day before yesterday, Zhong Jizhao, captain of the Public Security Bureau Detective Squad, received a confidential report that the bandits involved in the case, Tao Yalin and others, were hiding in a thatched shed in Dingjia Village near Hushu Pass in Suzhou. After receiving the report, Captain Zhong hired a motorboat and led detectives Dai Jingshan, Wang Bingsheng, and all the detectives, including Wu Bingkui, over ten people in total, to set off in the rain to make arrests according to the address. When they arrived at Dingjiaqiao Village in Suzhou, there were indeed two thatched houses. They entered to make arrests. At that time, the bandits Tao Yalin, Yu Rengen, Chen Heshang, and Zhu Zengfu were sitting around a table, deeply absorbed in a game of mahjong. They were all captured at once. A box cannon, a row of bullets, an old-fashioned front-loading gun were found under the pillows in their room. Matching the numbers, they were the same as the firearms lost by Chen's family. They were immediately taken to the boat for safekeeping and escorted to Wuxi. Captain Zhong interrogated them strictly. The criminals confessed to robbing Chen Xiangchun's home of firearms and gold and silver jewelry without denying it. Yesterday (12th), they were transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Zhenjiang: Spring Cocoons About to Come on the Market, Jiangsu Province Promulgates Protection Measures 65

The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that with the silk cocoons about to come on the market this year, all matters related to protecting the cocoon market should be planned as early as possible to facilitate implementation. It has formulated seven articles of protection measures with reference to previous cases, and ordered commissioners, county magistrates, and security regiment leaders to abide by them in order to ensure thoroughness. The protection measures are: The protection of the cocoon market should be jointly undertaken by the public security bureaus, security teams, and water police teams of various counties, as well as the garrison army. In the area along Taihu Lake in southern Jiangsu, the most prosperous area for the cocoon market, an office should be established in Wuxi County during the cocoon season to supervise and direct matters related to protecting the cocoon market in the region. The 1st District of the Water Police Team should dispatch ten patrol boats, and the Civil Affairs Department should also transfer several patrol warships, and all ships of the 2nd District of the Water Police Team to the office to meet the needs of cocoon merchants requesting protection and to be dispatched at any time. Wherever a cocoon market is established, the public security bureaus, security teams, or garrison troops of the respective counties should be stationed on land to protect it. The Water Police Team should dispatch ships to patrol and station at different locations. However, if there is no Water Police Team stationed within the territory of each county, all water patrol matters should still be the responsibility of the public security bureaus and security teams of the respective counties. For cocoon merchants transporting funds via land, each line along the route should dispatch police to escort them. For those traveling by waterway, the nearest Water Police Team should dispatch ships to escort them. For those traveling by both land and water, the county public security bureau and Water Police Team should take turns escorting them. However, all cocoon merchants should notify the number of funds, the starting and ending points of transportation, the places of handover, and the dates in advance for thoroughness. In important ports and prosperous areas of the cocoon market, the county public security bureau, the guaranteed-departure team, the garrison army, and the office should intensify the dispatch of troops and ships to patrol back and forth day and night to show caution. All military police responsible for protecting the cocoon market, regardless of officers or soldiers, must not solicit rewards from cocoon merchants. If there are any violations, cocoon merchants are allowed to report them for investigation at any time.

Nantong: Remedying the County's Financial Deficit 67

Nantong County is currently experiencing a period of sluggish tax revenue, making it difficult to disburse funds for various agencies. The county government and the financial industry have agreed that during the off-season, 15,000 yuan will be borrowed and allocated each month, with monthly interest of 8%, using the county tax as collateral for repayment at the end of the year. The county government has determined that the people owe over two million yuan in land tax. On the 11th, it finished investigating the grain declarations. From the 25th to the 31st, the entire county will launch a campaign to collect outstanding taxes, using the Baojia system to squeeze out the taxes.

The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, under orders to complete the Yongrui-Pingxiang highway project, is facing a severe shortage of funds. In addition to paying a security deposit of 100,000 yuan based on the length of the route, a percentage of 20-30% of the monthly operating income will be paid as rent. All the terms are currently under negotiation and are expected to be finalized and established within the month. The security deposit will be used for road construction.

Ningbo: Fishermen's Association Protests over National Assembly Representatives 70

The fishermen's associations of four counties in Yin District, Xiangshan, Dinghai, Yuhuan, and Linhai, believe that in the quota of representatives for the National Assembly promulgated this time, professional groups such as the agricultural, industrial, and commercial associations have been allocated, while the fishermen's associations, which account for a wide area in the seven provinces of the country and whose number accounts for one-tenth of the national population, have not been allocated any representatives. Therefore, they have jointly telegraphed the Central Government, requesting permission to participate.

Wuhu: Change of General Manager of the Electric Light Company 71

(Wuhu) After the death of Mr. Li Yanshi, the General Manager of the Mingyuan Electric Light Company, the Board of Directors decided to promote Mr. Shen Sifang, the chief engineer of the company, to the position of General Manager. He has served as the chief engineer of the Nanjing Power Plant and the Wuxing Electric Company, the director of the Wusong China Iron Works, the engineer of the Changzhou Zhenhua Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant, the China Electrical Company, and the Shanghai Great China Cotton Mill, a standing member of the National Private Electricity Association, and a professor at National Zhejiang University.
